SIGMOD conference: 2017: dataflow processing

What you need to know:

The SITES format can vary widely among systems. SITES data sets are a collection of files containing data in S/2012. When an endpoint is connected to a computer network and data is processed, it is called a data flow (DGR) to deliver that data. More info: https://tools.ietf.org/html/draft-5-dat	1
